At best Negligent - or worse Fraudulent - billing practices.

My wife and I went here as cash patients (we don't have vision coverage in our health plan) - and we paid our bill in full for our exams at the time of service.  They required our health insurance information for "their records" but said they would not use it because we were just getting routine annual exams.

we then get a bill from their office for $15 (apparently a co-pay?) where they submitted the same bills we paid for in CASH - in FULL - to our insurance company.  So either they erroneously submitted to the insurance company - or purposefully attempted to double-bill both US (cash patients) and the insurance company.

So we call them multiple times and leave messages; never get a call back.  Months go by - we still get notices for the $15 now past due - and we keep trying to call them to have them reverse the erroneous charges.  NO RESPONSE.

We then get the "red notice" saying they are sending this to collections.  We pay the $15 to simply avoid this stupid charge hitting our credit report.  Important to note - this $15 bill was FROM THIS CLINIC - and was NOT from our insurance company.  So if we were cash patients on the day - paid in full - why would they send us ANOTHER bill later on for $15 (and the bill shows they attempted to bill off against insurance etc).  This document is 100% entirely within their control (and as I confirmed with our insurance company) and this billing was not generated by our insurance company)

Needless to say - regardless of how "nice" their technology and how "high end" their practice is - when a business is non-responsive to fix such a simple issue like this - over many months - then the unethical nature of their billing (with us as their clients bearing the burden of chasing down the issues) - means I will NEVER go to this place again.   I'll also NEVER recommend anyone else go here - because if you do - their obvious efforts to double bill both cash patients and insurance companies will mean you will keep paying (with your time, or $$) for many months beyond the day you see a doctor.< /Text>

< username>
Dina Moody< /username>
<Time>1453773675024<//Time><rating>5<//rating>< text>
I've brought all of my dogs to Dr. Tisdale's office for their various needs. Recently, I adopted a new puppy and, funds being tight, I looked around for a better deal for his basic shot series with the intent of transferring him over to Dr. Tisdale after that set of four. My little guy is friendly and out-going but he did not like the bargain vet. By the second visit, he was tentative. By the third, he was hiding under my chair but I was able to coax him out. By his final visit, he was under the chair and I had a hard time getting him out until I headed for the door. As I was with him the whole time, I couldn't understand why he was uncomfortable. Granted, no one really played or introduced themselves to him but I didn't see anything to upset him. I was personally unhappy as I felt like I was being nickeled and dimed for every other service he might need. But, I expected this...

Fast forward to last week...my little guy and my big guy were playing and as sometimes happens they got a bit overexcited. I hear a crash and here comes my little guy with the "I didn't do it look" on his face. A few minutes later, I realize he is bleeding and needs stitches. So, of course, I call Dr. Tisdale's office. Shadow is going through a shy phase right now but he quickly warmed up to Dr. Tisdale's awesome staff and the new vet who easily won a few puppy kisses in no time! In less than an hour, he was awake, stitched and trying to escape his cone.

As I've always experienced with Dr. Tisdale's office, his staff was friendly toward me and, most importantly, toward my puppy. Already nervous, they took the few minutes to get acquainted with him that he needed and talked to him the whole time--even when he was asleep. They even made sure to ask that my big guy, Blue, was undamaged in the crash of glass. This is a first rate staff and one that tends to stick around...the vet techs have been there forever!! They remember my big guy and the one before him. You just can't ask for more than to have first rate care from your vet AND his staff but to have them like and care about your pets is amazing!!< /text>

As a vegetarian,  this food at this place is great!  I usually get half pad Thai,  half fried rice and a side of egg plant tofu.  They claim that there are no eggs or meat in any of those items, awesome!!

So why the two stars?  The lady that rang me up was unbelievable rude. I asked her for a couple of extra sriracha packets,  and she absolutely through a fit, saying they only give one and I don't need more. She said,  "are you serious!!?"  with a very disgusted and disturbed face.  I was baffled.  Over two sriracha packets?  Come on lady.

I'll probably go back,  but as far as reviews go,  two stars it is.<//Review>

<Text>Wish I caught the name of the sales associate who helped me -- they were phenomenal and I'm going to call the store after writing this review!

I've lived as both a small and large woman, and am now plus sized. As such, I've experienced a wide range of treatment: always warm when I was a size 6, but wildly ranging as my weight crept up.

Shopping the sparse plus sized department at this Nordstrom, I had a few items to try on. Because the associate in the plus department disappeared after greeting me, I had to seek out the associate in the kids department across the store. (Pretty common, as most department stores treat plus size retail and staffing as low priority). From the outset, they treated me warmly and didn't mention that they were now forced to cover a department that was not theirs. They promised to check on me in a few minutes, and actually did.

I found a pair of jeans I loved but was hoping to locate a jacket that was available in store according to the Nordstrom app but nowhere to be found in person. Not only did they perform the online stock search, showing me the results, but when it couldn't be found they asked if it was okay if they did a quick pass to scour the racks to locate it. Even though it was nowhere to be found and I was disappointed that I couldn't purchase the item, I was thrilled at their attentiveness, kindness, and enthusiasm to assist. Even though I spend about $5k+ at Nordstrom annually, most of that is spent online because of inadequate stock as well as a lack of service in the plus department. This associate is a model of service and I'm grateful for their expertise and kindness.<//Text><Pictures>None<//Pictures>< response>
None</response>

<rate>5< /rate>< review>
I just love Nordstrom, and especially the Nordstrom in downtown San Francisco.  It's five stories of heaven!  A one-stop shop for all your clothing and cosmetic needs.

One of my favorite parts about this location in particular is that they have a full cafe with a liquor license so they can make some amazing drinks to go with your meal.  My favorite is the blueberry fusion.  The Nordstrom Cafe is a great place to go whether you're looking for lunch or dinner.  Their menu is surprisingly good given that their primary focus is clothing.  They're always good about having sports on their TVs so it's a great escape for the not-so-into-shopping husband, too.

Nordstrom SF also has a spa with some amazing services including massages, facials, and lash extensions.  I prefer the Nordstrom Spa over most more well-known spas because it's much more intimate.<//review>

<Text>I personally don't shop at Nordstroms very often, but when I'm in San Francisco I always end up shopping and I usually end up here. To me it's one of the nicer locations. It's in a very busy mall with its own elevators to get to the main sections which also have their own escalators, albeit strange curved wrap around kind. A novelty. The mens section which is always just about half of 1 level is well stocked with quality clothing. I usually just pick up accent pieces to complete things rather than stock up on basics due to price. For some reason I like buying dress shoes here and button up shirts. I generally feel they cater to a more fashionable men's crowd and don't try to be too hip. No skinny jeans here people. I get my collar stays here because they are brass, certain accessories every man should have as well. I actually just pick up 1 or two items here and not shop shop.

It's clean the staff is friendly and helpful. I feel like down in hometown of San Diego they care more about their flip flops and aren't about the good shoes (kicks don't count). I'm not a shoe guy either, but when you have a nice pair of shoes outlast a dozen cheaper pairs it's nice.

Usually the caf√©'s in Nordstrom's are very good, not amazing, but good. I kind of expected more from them, but that I'll save for a separate review. Clean bathrooms, but mostly tourists come in to use the child changing tables and the facilities because they are much nicer than most around.

Price is high, even for the city and other Nordstroms around. They have great lighting and minimal decorations. Staff is not just a bunch of people working there for the discounts either.<//Text><gmap_id>0x80858085e669cca1:0xd929252f6c42706e</gmap_id><username>Walter Macalma< /username>< Pics>
